PROMPT == Step 4. EXISTING_ITEM + DEAL_RECORD (1:1, showcase limit applied) ==

DECLARE
    c_players   NUMBER;
    v_player    NUMBER;
    v_seller    NUMBER;
    v_buyer     NUMBER;
    v_item_id   NUMBER;
    v_icat      NUMBER;
    v_base      NUMBER;
    v_fraud     NUMBER;
    v_wc        NUMBER;
    v_clumsy    NUMBER;
    v_grade     NUMBER;
    v_flaws     NUMBER;
    v_auth      CHAR(1);
    v_found_grade NUMBER;
    v_found_flaw  NUMBER;
    v_found_auth  CHAR(1);
    v_asking    NUMBER;
    v_purchase  NUMBER;
    v_appraised NUMBER;
    v_selling   NUMBER;
    v_isactive  CHAR(1);
    v_sold_day  NUMBER;
    v_counterfeit_prob NUMBER;
    v_grade_factor     NUMBER;
    v_item_state NUMBER;
    v_max_showcase NUMBER;

    TYPE showcase_counter IS TABLE OF NUMBER INDEX BY PLS_INTEGER;
    v_showcase showcase_counter;
BEGIN
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO c_players FROM PLAYER;

    FOR i IN 1..1500 LOOP
        v_player := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(1, 201));
        v_seller := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(1, 101));

        SELECT UNLOCKED_SHOWCASE_COUNT INTO v_max_showcase FROM PLAYER WHERE PLR_KEY = v_player;
        IF NOT v_showcase.EXISTS(v_player) THEN
            v_showcase(v_player) := 0;
        END IF;

        v_icat := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(1, 101));
        SELECT BASE_PRICE INTO v_base FROM ITEM_CATALOG WHERE ICT_KEY = v_icat;

        SELECT FRAUD, WELL_COLLECT, CLUMSY
          INTO v_fraud, v_wc, v_clumsy
          FROM CUSTOMER WHERE CUS_KEY = v_seller;

        v_grade := CASE
                      WHEN DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,1) < (0.35 + (0.65*(1-v_wc))/3) THEN 0
                      WHEN DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,1) < (0.65 + (0.65*(1-v_wc))/3) THEN 1
                      WHEN DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,1) < (0.85 + (0.65*(1-v_wc))/3) THEN 2
                      ELSE 3
                   END;

        v_flaws := ROUND((10 * v_clumsy) + (4 * DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,1)));
        IF v_flaws > 14 THEN v_flaws := 14; END IF;

        v_auth := CASE WHEN DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,1) < (10 + 90 * v_fraud)/100 THEN 'N' ELSE 'Y' END;

        v_found_grade := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0, v_grade + 1));
        v_found_flaw  := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0, v_flaws + 1));
        IF DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,1) < 0.4 THEN
            v_found_auth := NULL;
        ELSE
            v_found_auth := v_auth;
        END IF;

        v_counterfeit_prob := 10 + 90 * v_fraud;
        v_grade_factor := (1 + 0.3 * v_grade) / 3;
        v_asking := v_base
                  * (1 - 0.02 * v_flaws)
                  * (1 - 0.3 * (v_counterfeit_prob/100))
                  * v_grade_factor
                  * (1 + 0.25 * v_fraud)
                  * (1 + 0.2 * (v_wc - 0.5));

        IF v_asking < 0 THEN v_asking := 0; END IF;
        v_purchase  := v_asking;
        v_appraised := v_asking;

        IF v_auth = 'N' THEN
            v_purchase  := v_purchase  * 0.5;
            v_appraised := v_appraised * 0.8;
        END IF;

        CASE v_grade
            WHEN 3 THEN v_appraised := GREATEST(v_appraised, v_asking * 1.7);
            WHEN 2 THEN v_appraised := GREATEST(v_appraised, v_asking * 1.5);
            WHEN 1 THEN v_appraised := GREATEST(v_appraised, v_asking * 1.2);
            ELSE NULL;
        END CASE;

        -- Showcase limit check
        IF v_showcase(v_player) >= v_max_showcase THEN
            v_isactive := 'N';
            v_item_state := 4;
            LOOP
                v_buyer := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(1, 101));
                EXIT WHEN v_buyer <> v_seller;
            END LOOP;
            v_sold_day := TRUNC(DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(1, 201));
            v_selling := ROUND(v_appraised * 0.8);
        ELSE
            v_isactive := 'Y';
            v_buyer := NULL;
            v_sold_day := NULL;
            v_selling := NULL;  -- ✅ unsold → NULL
            v_item_state := 1;
            v_showcase(v_player) := v_showcase(v_player) + 1;
        END IF;

        INSERT INTO EXISTING_ITEM (
            PLAYER_KEY, ICAT_KEY,
            GRADE, FOUND_GRADE,
            FLAW_EA, FOUND_FLAW_EA,
            AUTHENTICITY, FOUND_AUTHENTICITY,
            ITEM_STATE, ISACTIVE
        )
        VALUES (
            v_player, v_icat,
            v_grade, v_found_grade,
            v_flaws, v_found_flaw,
            v_auth, v_found_auth,
            v_item_state, 'Y'
        )
        RETURNING ITM_KEY INTO v_item_id;

        INSERT INTO DEAL_RECORD (
            PLAYER_KEY, SELLER_KEY, BUYER_KEY, ITEM_KEY,
            ASKING_PRICE, PURCHASE_PRICE, APPRAISED_PRICE, SELLING_PRICE,
            ISACTIVE, SOLD_DATE
        )
        VALUES (
            v_player, v_seller, v_buyer, v_item_id,
            ROUND(v_asking),
            ROUND(v_purchase),
            ROUND(v_appraised),
            ROUND(v_selling),  -- NULL 유지됨
            v_isactive,
            v_sold_day
        );
    END LOOP;
END;
/
COMMIT;

PROMPT == Step 6. PLAYER_ITEM_DISPLAY (ongoing items only) ==
DECLARE
  CURSOR c_plr IS
    SELECT PLR_KEY, UNLOCKED_SHOWCASE_COUNT FROM PLAYER;
  v_taken NUMBER;
BEGIN
  FOR r IN c_plr LOOP
    SELECT COUNT(*) INTO v_taken
      FROM PLAYER_ITEM_DISPLAY
     WHERE PLAYER_KEY = r.PLR_KEY;

    FOR rec IN (
      SELECT d.ITEM_KEY,
             ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY d.DRC_KEY) - 1 AS pos
        FROM DEAL_RECORD d
        JOIN EXISTING_ITEM ei ON ei.ITM_KEY = d.ITEM_KEY
       WHERE d.PLAYER_KEY = r.PLR_KEY
         AND d.ISACTIVE = 'Y'
         AND ei.ITEM_STATE = 1
         AND NOT EXISTS (
               SELECT 1 FROM PLAYER_ITEM_DISPLAY pid
                WHERE pid.PLAYER_KEY = r.PLR_KEY
                  AND pid.ITEM_KEY   = d.ITEM_KEY
             )
       FETCH FIRST GREATEST(0, r.UNLOCKED_SHOWCASE_COUNT - v_taken) ROWS ONLY
    ) LOOP
      BEGIN
        INSERT INTO PLAYER_ITEM_DISPLAY (PLAYER_KEY, ITEM_KEY, DISPLAY_POS)
        VALUES (r.PLR_KEY, rec.ITEM_KEY, MOD(rec.pos, 8));
      EXCEPTION WHEN DUP_VAL_ON_INDEX THEN NULL;
      END;
    END LOOP;
  END LOOP;
END;
/

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PROMPT == Step 8. EXISTING_NEWS (weekly global events; replace all every 7 days) ==
DECLARE
  v_news_cnt NUMBER;
  v_n NUMBER;
  v_k NUMBER;
  v_amt NUMBER;
BEGIN
  SELECT COUNT(*) INTO v_news_cnt FROM NEWS_CATALOG;

  FOR r IN (SELECT PLR_KEY, DAY_COUNT FROM PLAYER) LOOP
    -- 1~6일차는 뉴스 없음, 7의 배수일(7,14,21,...)부터는 항상 뉴스 유지
    IF r.DAY_COUNT >= 7 THEN
      -- 기존 뉴스 삭제
      DELETE FROM EXISTING_NEWS WHERE PLAYER_KEY = r.PLR_KEY;

      -- 플레이어별 1~3개 뉴스 생성
      v_n := rnd_int(1,3);
      FOR i IN 1..v_n LOOP
        v_k := rnd_int(1, v_news_cnt);
        v_amt := rnd_int(1, 50); -- 영향 강도 (양수)
        INSERT INTO EXISTING_NEWS (PLAYER_KEY, NCAT_KEY, AMOUNT)
        VALUES (r.PLR_KEY, v_k, v_amt);
      END LOOP;
    END IF;
  END LOOP;
END;
/

PROMPT == Step 9. WORLD_RECORD (all finished deals recorded; no per-player limit) ==
INSERT INTO WORLD_RECORD (PLAYER_KEY, CLEAR_DAY_COUNT, CLEAR_DATE, LGST_PROFIT_DEAL_KEY)
SELECT dr.PLAYER_KEY,
       rnd_int(30,300),
       SYSDATE - DBMS_RANDOM.VALUE(0,300),
       dr.DRC_KEY
  FROM DEAL_RECORD dr
 WHERE dr.ISACTIVE = 'N';
/

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

PROMPT == Done. Verify counts ==

SELECT TBL, CNT
FROM (
  SELECT 'PLAYER' AS TBL, COUNT(*) AS CNT FROM PLAYER
  UNION ALL SELECT 'CUSTOMER', COUNT(*) FROM CUSTOMER
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ITEM_CATEGORY', COUNT(*) FROM ITEM_CATEGORY
  UNION ALL SELECT 'ITEM_CATALOG', COUNT(*) FROM ITEM_CATALOG
  UNION ALL SELECT 'EXISTING_ITEM', COUNT(*) FROM EXISTING_ITEM
  UNION ALL SELECT 'DEAL_RECORD', COUNT(*) FROM DEAL_RECORD
  UNION ALL SELECT 'PCHD (HIDDEN)', COUNT(*) FROM PLAYER_CUSTOMER_HIDDEN_DISCOVERED
  UNION ALL SELECT 'DISPLAY', COUNT(*) FROM PLAYER_ITEM_DISPLAY
  UNION ALL SELECT 'WORLD_RECORD', COUNT(*) FROM WORLD_RECORD
  UNION ALL SELECT 'LOAN', COUNT(*) FROM LOAN
  UNION ALL SELECT 'EXISTING_NEWS', COUNT(*) FROM EXISTING_NEWS
  UNION ALL SELECT 'NEWS_CATALOG', COUNT(*) FROM NEWS_CATALOG
  UNION ALL SELECT 'LOGIN_LOG', COUNT(*) FROM LOGIN_LOG
)
UNION ALL
SELECT 'TOTAL', SUM(CNT)
FROM (
  SELECT COUNT(*) AS CNT FROM PLAYER
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM EXISTING_ITEM
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM DEAL_RECORD
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM PLAYER_CUSTOMER_HIDDEN_DISCOVERED
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM PLAYER_ITEM_DISPLAY
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM LOAN
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM LOGIN_LOG
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM EXISTING_NEWS
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM WORLD_RECORD
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ITEM_CATALOG
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM NEWS_CATALOG
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM CUSTOMER
  UNION ALL SELECT COUNT(*) FROM ITEM_CATEGORY
);
